# Fine-Grained Implementation Tracker - AppPlatform Multi-Domain Operating System

**Version**: 1.0.0  
**Date**: March 13, 2026  
**Status**: Operational tracking document  
**Derived From**: `WEEK_BY_WEEK_IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md`, `UNIFIED_IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md`, `stories/STORY_INDEX.md`, milestone story files, `epics/DEPENDENCY_MATRIX.md`, and `tdd_spec_phase0_bootstrap_v2.1.md`

## 1. Purpose

This document turns the implementation plan into a working tracker for day-to-day delivery. It is not a new authority source: the backlog, acceptance criteria, tests, dependencies, reuse rules, and sprint ordering remain governed by the source documents listed above. Use this file to track execution status, ownership, evidence, blockers, and carryover without losing traceability back to the authoritative plan and story files.

## 2. How To Use This Tracker

- Update every row in place; do not create shadow trackers per team or sprint.
- Keep the story rows operational: set `Status`, fill `Owner`, and append links or notes in `Validation / Evidence` as work progresses.
- Treat the story description, dependencies, and listed tests as the minimum expected scope. Full acceptance criteria remain in the linked milestone story file.
- A story cannot move to `DONE` until the relevant Definition of Ready, Definition of Done, sprint gates, and quality gates are satisfied.
- If a dependency, LLD, contract, or environment prerequisite is missing, mark the row `BLK` and log the blocker explicitly in `Validation / Evidence`.

**Status Legend**

- `NS`: Not started
- `RDY`: Ready: all Definition of Ready checks complete
- `WIP`: Implementation in progress
- `BLK`: Blocked by dependency, environment, or design gap
- `RVW`: In review / awaiting validation or sign-off
- `DONE`: Definition of Done and sprint gates satisfied

## 3. Global Story Expectations

Every story row in this tracker inherits the expectations below from the week-by-week plan and related authority documents.

| Expectation Area                | What Must Be True Before The Story Can Close                                                                                                                            |
| ------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Definition of Ready             | Story ID, milestone file, epic, LLD or documented gap, TDD reference, reuse decision, dependency confirmation, and changed contracts are identified before work starts. |
| Contract-first execution        | Week 1 finalizes APIs, events, schemas, config, workflow metadata, audit points, and observability before broad implementation.                                         |
| Testing                         | Story-level tests from the milestone file are written or updated first and pass at the correct layer per the TDD master index.                                          |
| Audit                           | K-07 audit path exists for every state-changing workflow and evidence of coverage is linked in the story row.                                                           |
| Observability                   | K-06 logs, metrics, traces, alerts, and dashboards are added where the story changes runtime behavior.                                                                  |
| Configuration                   | Variable behavior routes through K-02; no hardcoded jurisdiction, threshold, or pack behavior.                                                                          |
| Reuse decision                  | Ghatana reuse is logged as reuse, extend, or net-new with rationale and artifact path.                                                                                  |
| Security and dependency hygiene | SAST, dependency audit, secret scanning, and container/image checks pass for changed scope.                                                                             |
| Performance and resilience      | Run the relevant baseline, latency, throughput, replay, rollback, or failover checks when the story affects those NFRs.                                                 |
| Documentation and traceability  | Touched docs, source-register, legal-citation, and claim-traceability files are updated in the same change when language or market facts change.                        |
| Code quality and standards      | Spotless, checkstyle/PMD, JavaDoc `@doc.*` tags, async test conventions, and link integrity checks all pass.                                                            |

## 7. Detailed Story Ledger By Sprint

The detailed sections below preserve sprint focus, source bundles, exit gates, and every story assigned to that sprint. Update `Validation / Evidence` with PR links, CI runs, benchmark output, security evidence, demo links, and carryover notes.

### Sprint 1

**Dates**: March 9 - March 20, 2026  
**Focus**: K-05 core bus/event store plus K-07 bootstrap audit path  
**Story Load**: 24 stories / 65 story points  
**Exit Gate**: K-05 append/publish path works and K-07 synchronous audit bootstrap is live  
**Primary Source Set**: `stories/MILESTONE_1A_STORIES.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-05-Event-Bus.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-07-Audit-Framework.md`, `lld/LLD_K05_EVENT_BUS.md`, `lld/LLD_K07_AUDIT_FRAMEWORK.md`, `tdd_spec_k05_event_bus_expanded_v2.1.md`, `tdd_spec_k07_audit_framework_expanded_v2.1.md`, `../finance-ghatana-integration-plan.md` §5.1

### Sprint 2

**Dates**: March 23 - April 3, 2026  
**Focus**: Close K-05/K-07 bootstrap cycle, deliver K-02 hierarchy and K-15 calendar core  
**Story Load**: 54 stories / 147 story points  
**Exit Gate**: K-05 to K-07 audit hook enabled, config hierarchy works, calendar correctness suite passes  
**Primary Source Set**: `stories/MILESTONE_1A_STORIES.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-02-Configuration-Engine.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-15-Dual-Calendar-Service.md`, `lld/LLD_K02_CONFIGURATION_ENGINE.md`, `lld/LLD_K15_DUAL_CALENDAR.md`, `tdd_spec_k02_configuration_engine_expanded_v2.1.md`, `tdd_spec_k15_dual_calendar_v2.1.md`, `../finance-ghatana-integration-plan.md` §5.1 (K-02: 70% reuse; K-15: net contributor back to Ghatana)

### Sprint 3

**Dates**: April 6 - April 17, 2026  
**Focus**: Sprint 3 first slices: K-01 and K-14 plus initial K-06, K-11, K-16, K-17, and K-18 work  
**Story Load**: 47 stories / 123 story points  
**Exit Gate**: Early auth, secrets, observability, gateway, ledger, DTC, and resilience slices are stable enough for Sprint 4 completion work  
**Primary Source Set**: `stories/MILESTONE_1B_STORIES.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-01-IAM.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-14-Secrets-Management.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-06-Observability.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-11-API-Gateway.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-16-Ledger-Framework.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-17-Distributed-Transaction-Coordinator.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-18-Resilience-Patterns.md`, `lld/LLD_K01_IAM.md`, `lld/LLD_K14_SECRETS_MANAGEMENT.md`, `lld/LLD_K06_OBSERVABILITY.md`, `lld/LLD_K11_API_GATEWAY.md`, `lld/LLD_K16_LEDGER_FRAMEWORK.md`, `lld/LLD_K17_DISTRIBUTED_TRANSACTION_COORDINATOR.md`, `lld/LLD_K18_RESILIENCE_PATTERNS.md`, `epics/DEPENDENCY_MATRIX.md`, `tdd_spec_phase2_kernel_completion_v2.1.md`, `../finance-ghatana-integration-plan.md` §5.1 (K-06: ~100%, K-18: 90%, K-11: 80% reuse)

**Dates**: April 20 - May 1, 2026  
**Focus**: Sprint 4 completion: finish M1B, complete remaining K-01/K-14 work, and add K-03/K-04 without duplicating earlier kernel work  
**Story Load**: 100 stories / 246 story points  
**Exit Gate**: Core kernel readiness gates met for domain-pack consumption

| `DONE`   |       | `STORY-K06-022` Implement intelligent alert noise reduction and event correlation | Alpha / 5                  | STORY-K06-018, K-08 (lineage graph), K-09 (AI governance — K09-004)              | Reduce alert noise via ML alert grouping, deduplication, and root cause inference. Grouping: alerts within a 5-minute sliding window across correlated services (dependency graph from K-08 lineage) merged into a single incident entity. Deduplication: embedding-similarity dedup (cosine > 0.92 = same alert). Root cause inference: graph traversal of K-08 service dependency graph + temporal ordering to propose likely root cause service. Suppression: if 80%+ of alerts are downstream symptoms of one root cause, suppress children and surface root cause only. Result: SRE sees one correlated incident with root cause hypothesis vs dozens of raw alert notifications. All correlation logic governed and explainable via K-09. | Tests: alert_grouping_5min_window · dedup_embedding_similarity · root_cause_inference · symptom_suppression · dependency_graph_traversal · shap_explanation · perf_correlation_under_5sec · flapping_detection         | `stories/MILESTONE_1B_STORIES.md`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |

### Sprint 5

**Dates**: May 4 - May 15, 2026  
**Focus**: D-11 reference data, D-04 market data, D-01 OMS tracer bullet  
**Story Load**: 16 stories / 43 story points  
**Exit Gate**: Reference data, market data, and OMS first order flow integrate through K-05/K-03/K-16  
**Primary Source Set**: `stories/MILESTONE_2A_STORIES.md`, `epics/EPIC-D-11-Reference-Data.md`, `epics/EPIC-D-04-Market-Data.md`, `epics/EPIC-D-01-OMS.md`, `lld/LLD_D11_REFERENCE_DATA.md`, `lld/LLD_D04_MARKET_DATA.md`, `lld/LLD_D01_OMS.md`, `tdd_spec_d01_oms_expanded_v2.1.md`, `tdd_spec_phase3_trading_mvp_v2.1.md`, `INTER_DOMAIN_PACK_COMMUNICATION_SPEC.md`, `DOMAIN_PACK_INTERFACE_SPECIFICATION.md`, `../finance-ghatana-integration-plan.md` §3.1 (AEP for event processing), §3.2 (Data Cloud for reference data)

**Dates**: May 18 - May 29, 2026

**Dates**: August 10 - August 21, 2026

### Sprint 13

**Dates**: August 24 - September 4, 2026  
**Focus**: Sprint 13 first slices across K-13, K-12, W-01, and W-02. **LLD creation gate**: W-01 and W-02 LLDs must be authored in Week 1 (see §4.3)  
**Story Load**: 24 stories / 68 story points  
**Exit Gate**: Admin, SDK, workflow, and onboarding first slices are integrated without duplicating control-plane behavior; W-01 and W-02 LLDs delivered  
**Primary Source Set**: `stories/MILESTONE_3B_STORIES.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-13-Admin-Portal.md`, `epics/EPIC-K-12-Platform-SDK.md`, `epics/EPIC-W-01-Workflow-Orchestration.md`, `epics/EPIC-W-02-Client-Onboarding.md`, `lld/LLD_K13_ADMIN_PORTAL.md`, `lld/LLD_K12_PLATFORM_SDK.md`, `EXTENSION_POINT_CATALOG.md`, `tdd_spec_phase2_kernel_completion_v2.1.md`, `tdd_spec_phase4_5_operational_hardening_v2.1.md`, `../finance-ghatana-integration-plan.md` §5.1 (K-12 SDK: 100% composition of platform artifacts)

Step types: TASK (execute microservice call), DECISION (conditional branch), PARALLEL (concurrent steps), WAIT (delay or event), SUB_WORKFLOW. Stored in PostgreSQL with full version history. **Dates**: September 7 - September 18, 2026

### Sprint 18

**Dates**: November 2 - November 13, 2026

## 8. Completion Rules Reference

Use the source plan for full text, but do not mark work complete until the following are true:

- The story acceptance criteria in the milestone file are met.
- Relevant epic and LLD contracts are implemented or updated, or the documented LLD-gap process is satisfied.
- Tests pass at the required layer and ARB coverage remains intact.
- Reuse decisions, JavaDoc tags, async-test conventions, style checks, SAST, dependency audit, and link integrity checks are all complete.
- Documentation, traceability artifacts, and deferred-risk notes are updated in the same change.
